 galakat pratiyogita vaali pravesh pariksha main kaamyaab hone ke baad desh ke 8 pramukh bhartiya praudyogiki sansthaanon (iaiti) main daakhila paane vaale kareeb 66,000 vidhyaarthee faikalti ke abhaav se jujh rahe hai
 This information has been disclosed by the Right to Information (RTI)
 jisamen bataaya gaya he ki desh ke 8 pramukh bhartiya praudyogiki sansthaanon main ausat aadhaar par shikshakon ke lagbhag 36 pratishat sweekrut pad khaali pade hai
 RTI activist Chandrashekhar Gaur, resident of Neemuch in Madhya Pradesh, told the news agency that in response to his application, a top official of the Union Human Resource Development Ministry has given this information to him in a letter sent to him on 26 November
 artiai ke tahat muhaiyaa karaae gaye aankade bataate hai ki mumbai (bombai), dilli, guwahati, kanpur, khadgpur, chennai (madras), rudki or varanasi sthit iaiti main philhal 65,824 vidhyaarthee pard rahe hai
 According to the government report, the number of teachers teaching in these iits is more than 4,049 vacancies in IIT, while a total of 6,318 posts of faculty are approved
 yani 2,269 pad khaali rahane ke kaaran in sansthaanon main kareeb 36 pratishat shikshakon kii kami he
 The student-teacher ratio in these eight institutions is 16: 1 on an average basis
 yani vahaan har 16 vidhyaarthiyon par ek shikshak niyukt he
 The most serious situation of teacher shortage is at IIT BHU in Varanasi, where 5,485 students are studying in different courses
 is pratishthit santhaan main 548 sweekrut padon ke mukaable keval 265 shikshak kaam kar rahe hai
 This means that 283 posts of teachers are lying vacant in this institute and this figure shows a decrease of about 52 percent compared to the sanctioned posts
 is santhaan main har 21 vidhyaarthiyon par ek shikshak he

 This year, Makar Sakranti will be celebrated all over the country on 15 January
 aamtaur par yah tyohaar 14 janvari ke din hi manaaya jaataa he lekin is baar yah 15 janvari ko pad rahaa he
 Makar Sankranti is a special festival of Sun worship
 is din se surya uttarayan hona shuru hote hai or iske baad baad se dharti ke uttari golardh main sheet ritu kii thandak main kami aani shuru hoti he
 It is believed that on the day of Makar Sankranti, the Sun enters Capricorn except Sagittarius
 isi vajah se is sankranti ko makar sankranti ke naam se janaa jaataa he
 On Makar Sankranti, it is considered auspicious to worship your favorite deity along with sun worship
 makar sakranti ke din kis samay punyakaal muhoort or mahapunyakaal muhoort he or iske saath hi or is tyohaar main kis rajya main kya pakwaan banaae jate hai aaj ham aapako iske bare main bataaenge
 Punyakal Muhurta = 20 in the morning from 20 in the morning to 12 in the afternoon
 ( 15 janvari)avadhi= 5 ghante 19 minute
 Sakranti = 8 pm 5 pm on January 14
 mahapunyakaal muhoort= subah 7 bajkar 20 minute se raat 9 bajkar 7 minute tak
 (15 January) Duration = 1 hour 46 minutes
